\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em bcm2835\+S\+P\+I\+Clock\+Divider Specifies the divider used to generate the S\+PI clock from the system clock. Figures below give the divider, clock period and clock frequency. Clock divided is based on nominal core clock rate of 250M\+Hz on R\+Pi1 and R\+Pi2, and 400M\+Hz on R\+Pi3. It is reported that (contrary to the documentation) any even divider may used. The frequencies shown for each divider have been confirmed by measurement on R\+Pi1 and R\+Pi2. The system clock frequency on R\+Pi3 is different, so the frequency you get from a given divider will be different. See comments in \textquotesingle{}S\+PI Pins\textquotesingle{} for information about reliable S\+PI speeds. Note\+: it is possible to change the core clock rate of the R\+Pi 3 back to 250M\+Hz, by putting \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The values here are designed to be passed to various functions in the bcm2835 library.

\index{Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}!bcm2835SPIClockDivider@{bcm2835SPIClockDivider}}
\index{bcm2835SPIClockDivider@{bcm2835SPIClockDivider}!Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bcm2835SPIClockDivider}{bcm2835SPIClockDivider}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{group__constants_gaf2e0ca069b8caef24602a02e8a00884e}{bcm2835\+S\+P\+I\+Clock\+Divider}}}



bcm2835\+S\+P\+I\+Clock\+Divider Specifies the divider used to generate the S\+PI clock from the system clock. Figures below give the divider, clock period and clock frequency. Clock divided is based on nominal core clock rate of 250M\+Hz on R\+Pi1 and R\+Pi2, and 400M\+Hz on R\+Pi3. It is reported that (contrary to the documentation) any even divider may used. The frequencies shown for each divider have been confirmed by measurement on R\+Pi1 and R\+Pi2. The system clock frequency on R\+Pi3 is different, so the frequency you get from a given divider will be different. See comments in \textquotesingle{}S\+PI Pins\textquotesingle{} for information about reliable S\+PI speeds. Note\+: it is possible to change the core clock rate of the R\+Pi 3 back to 250M\+Hz, by putting 


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{core\_freq=250}
\end{DoxyCode}
 in the config.\+txt \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{BCM2835\_SPI\_CLOCK\_DIVIDER\_65536@{BCM2835\_SPI\_CLOCK\_DIVIDER\_65536}!Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}}\index{Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}!BCM2835\_SPI\_CLOCK\_DIVIDER\_65536@{BCM2835\_SPI\_CLOCK\_DIVIDER\_65536}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__constants_ggaf2e0ca069b8caef24602a02e8a00884eaa381b689cf30ac842a243a23bdf3309c}\label{group__constants_ggaf2e0ca069b8caef24602a02e8a00884eaa381b689cf30ac842a243a23bdf3309c}}

\index{Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}!RPiGPIOPin@{RPiGPIOPin}}
\index{RPiGPIOPin@{RPiGPIOPin}!Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{RPiGPIOPin}{RPiGPIOPin}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{group__constants_ga63c029bd6500167152db4e57736d0939}{R\+Pi\+G\+P\+I\+O\+Pin}}}



G\+P\+IO Pin Numbers. 

Here we define Raspberry Pin G\+P\+IO pins on P1 in terms of the underlying B\+CM G\+P\+IO pin numbers. These can be passed as a pin number to any function requiring a pin. Not all pins on the R\+Pi 26 bin I\+DE plug are connected to G\+P\+IO pins and some can adopt an alternate function. R\+Pi version 2 has some slightly different pinouts, and these are values R\+P\+I\+\_\+\+V2\+\_\+$\ast$. R\+Pi B+ has yet differnet pinouts and these are defined in R\+P\+I\+\_\+\+B\+P\+L\+U\+S\+\_\+$\ast$. At bootup, pins 8 and 10 are set to U\+A\+R\+T0\+\_\+\+T\+XD, U\+A\+R\+T0\+\_\+\+R\+XD (ie the alt0 function) respectively When S\+P\+I0 is in use (ie after \mbox{\hyperlink{group__spi_ga6f0330a183f3c5765a36f1839e029a44}{bcm2835\+\_\+spi\+\_\+begin()}}), S\+P\+I0 pins are dedicated to S\+PI and cant be controlled independently. If you are using the R\+Pi Compute Module, just use the G\+P\+IO number\+: there is no need to use one of these symbolic names \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_03@{RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_03}!Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}}\index{Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}!RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_03@{RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_03}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__constants_gga63c029bd6500167152db4e57736d0939a1517b7c4655c6717f16b83effd033a9e}\label{group__constants_gga63c029bd6500167152db4e57736d0939a1517b7c4655c6717f16b83effd033a9e}} 
R\+P\+I\+\_\+\+G\+P\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P1\+\_\+03&Version 1, Pin P1-\/03 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_05@{RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_05}!Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}}\index{Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}!RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_05@{RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_05}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__constants_gga63c029bd6500167152db4e57736d0939a8afeaa60595130f2b2a59428fac39bb9}\label{group__constants_gga63c029bd6500167152db4e57736d0939a8afeaa60595130f2b2a59428fac39bb9}} 
R\+P\+I\+\_\+\+G\+P\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P1\+\_\+05&Version 1, Pin P1-\/05 \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_07@{RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_07}!Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}}\index{Constants for passing to and from library functions@{Constants for passing to and from library functions}!RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_07@{RPI\_GPIO\_P1\_07}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__constants_gga63c029bd6500167152db4e57736d0939a41799c767a7a63811b6ef58b0f9da904}\label{group__constants_gga63c029bd6500167152db4e57736d0939a41799c767a7a63811b6ef58b0f9da904}}
